Our goal is to open all safe squares in the quickest time possible!\r\n\r\nThe goal of the game is to uncover all the squares that do not contain mines without being \"destroyed\" by clicking on a mine. The location of the mines is discovered by a process of logic. Some squares are blank but some contain numbers (1 to 8), each number being the number of mines adjacent to the uncovered square. To help avoid hitting a mine, the location of a suspected mine can be marked by flagging it with the right mouse button.
